. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. ** Temperature above 1.5 degrees
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptable:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 2.5°C
>  or more are summarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2.5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Global carbon price suggested
. ** Logarithmic form of suggested carbon prices
. gen ln_carbon_price = ln(carbon_price + 1)

. label var ln_carbon_price "Natural logarithm of suggested carbon_price"

. 
. ** Cropping carbon price suggested at 500 for visualization in figure 1a
. gen carbon_price_cap = carbon_price

. replace carbon_price_cap  = 501 if carbon_price > 500
(23 real changes made)

. egen mean_carbon_price = mean(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. egen median_carbon_price = median(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. tab temp_rise_cropped , gen(tr)

  All those |
 suggesting |
2.5 or more |
  collected |
     in 2.5 |      Freq.     Percent        Cum.
------------+-----------------------------------
          0 |         22        7.94        7.94
         .5 |         36       13.00       20.94
          1 |         42       15.16       36.10
        1.5 |        116       41.88       77.98
          2 |         40       14.44       92.42
        2.5 |         21        7.58      100.00
------------+-----------------------------------
      Total |        277      100.00

. 
. ** Price suggested below 60 USD
. gen price_below = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace price_below = 0 if carbon_price >= 60 
(126 real changes made)

. replace price_below = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below "Price suggested < USD60"

. 
. /*
> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices to stay below 
> a certain temperature rise. In the main paper we use USD60 as thte threshold. 
> As robustness test, we also test against other specifications.
> */
. gen price_below_60 = 0

. replace price_below_60 = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_60 "Price below USD60 suggested"

. 
. gen price_below_185 = 0

. replace price_below_185 = 1 if carbon_price < 185 
(224 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_185 "Price below USD185 suggested"

. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Region- and time-specific carbon price suggestions
. ** Logarithms of prices suggested prices for home, OECD, LDC / now, future
. foreach var in price_home_now price_oecd_now price_ldc_now price_home_future p
> rice_oecd_future price_ldc_future {
  2. gen ln_`var' = log(`var' + 1)
  3. }

. lab var ln_price_home_now "Ln of Price Home Now"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_now "Ln of Price OECD Now"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_now "Ln of Price LDCs Now"

. lab var ln_price_home_future "Ln of Price Home Future"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_future "Ln of Price OECD Future"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_future "Ln of Price LDCs Future"

. 
. ** Categorizing the ambitions of delegates for prices now and in the future
. gen ambition_home_fut = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 1 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future < 60
>   // Low ambition
(148 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 2 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future >= 6
> 0 // Shift to future
(50 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 3 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future < 60
>   // Shift to now
(3 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 4 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future >= 6
> 0 // High ambition
(76 real changes made)

. lab define ambition_fut 1 "Low ambition" 2 "Future pay more" 3 "Now pay more" 
> 4 "High ambition", replace

. lab val ambition_home_fut ambition_fut

. 
. 
. 
. // Mindset PCAs
. ** MINDSET PCAs

. *----------
. *   FIGURE 1: Temperature rise deemed acceptable, carbon price suggested, and 
> negotiation strategy applied
. *---------
. 
. // Figure Settings
. * Text size
. global head     10 // Title

. global legend    8 // Legend

. global xytitle   8 // Axis title

. global xylab     8 // Scale label

. 
. 
. // Fig 1 A: Stripplot: Price and temperature rise 
. * Generate variable defining position of observations on x-axis
. egen carbon_price_rank = rank(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropped) unique

. egen temp_rise_cropped_freq = count(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. gen  temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 = temp_rise_cropped + (carbon_price_rank *.006)
>  - (temp_rise_cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. 
. * Save number of observations in locals
. forvalues i = 1/6 {
  2. sum ln_carbon_price if tr`i' == 1
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         22    3.323065    2.261287          0   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         36    3.722019    2.127395   .6931472   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         21    3.544467    1.325008   .6931472   6.908755

>                                   ///

> n_3')" "' 4 `" "1.5°C" "(n=`n_4')" "' 5 `" "2°C" "(n=`n_5')" "' 6 `" "{&ge}2.5
> °C" "(n=`n_6')" "' , labsize(2.5 pt))                                         
>        ///
> legend(order(1 "Observation" 2 "Mean" 3 "Median") size($legend pt) rows(3) pos
> (6) ring(1) region(fcolor(%40)))

> es)
. preserve

. *gen income_level = (income_level -5 ) * (-1)

. *lab val income_level income_level1
. 
. forvalues i = 1/4 {
  2. sum income_level if income_level == `i'
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         50           1           0          1          1

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         56           3           0          3          3

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         68           4           0          4          4

> e price_oecd_future price_ldc_future , by(income_level)

  2. rename `var'_now `var'1
  3. rename `var'_future `var'2
  4. }

(note: j = 1 2)

Data                               wide   ->   long
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                        4   ->       8
Number of variables                   7   ->       5
j variable (2 values)                     ->   now_future
xij variables:
                price_home1 price_home2   ->   price_home
                price_oecd1 price_oecd2   ->   price_oecd
                  price_ldc1 price_ldc2   ->   price_ldc
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

.

.

(4 real changes made)

. // Fig 1a: Stripplot: Price and temperature rise

> ique

. egen temp_rise_cropped_freq = count(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropp
> ed)

. gen  temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 = temp_rise_cropped + (carbon_price_rank *
> .006) - (temp_rise_cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. forvalues i = 1/6 {
  2. sum ln_carbon_price if tr`i' == 1
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)

-------------+---------------------------------------------------------

> gle))                                  ///

> \Donia_Delegates\8_Submission\analysis\scripts\02 - analysis.do"

. *--------------------------------------------------
. * Analysis.do
. *-------------------------------------------------
. 
. 
. 
. *********************************************************
. **********               STRUCTURE             **********
. *********************************************************
. /*
> Main Body:
> - Fig. 1: Descriptives
>         a) Carbon price and temperature rise
>         b) Shifting the burden
> 
> - Fig. 2: Inferential
>         a) Answers towards technological optimism items
>         b) Technological optimism mindset and temperature & prices sugges
> ted
> */
. 
. 
. use "$working_ANALYSIS\delegates_analysis.dta", clear

. 
. 
. 
. *----------
. *   FIGURE 1: Temperature rise deemed acceptable, carbon price suggested,
>  and negotiation strategy applied
. *---------
. // Figure Settings
. * Text size
. global head     10 // Title

. global legend    8 // Legend

. global xytitle   8 // Axis title

. global xylab     8 // Scale label

. 
. 
. // Fig 1a: Stripplot: Price and temperature rise 
. * Generate variable defining position of observations on x-axis
. egen carbon_price_rank = rank(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropped) un
> ique

. egen temp_rise_cropped_freq = count(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropp
> ed)

. gen  temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 = temp_rise_cropped + (carbon_price_rank *
> .006) - (temp_rise_cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. 
. * Save number of observations in locals
. forvalues i = 1/6 {
  2. sum ln_carbon_price if tr`i' == 1
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         22    3.323065    2.261287          0   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         36    3.722019    2.127395   .6931472   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         42    4.207788    1.800718   1.098612   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |        116    4.121002    1.359837          0   7.313887

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         40    3.659859    1.407166          0   6.552508

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         21    3.544467    1.325008   .6931472   6.908755

. twoway ///
> (scatter carbon_price_cap temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 , mcolor(%30) msize(m
> edium) msymbol(o))              ///
> (scatter mean_carbon_price temp_rise_cropped , mcolor(538g) msymbol(trian
> gle))                                  ///
> (scatter median_carbon_price temp_rise_cropped , mcolor(538r) msymbol(squ
> are))                                  ///
> , title("{bf:a }", pos(11) span size($head pt))                          
>                                 ///
> ytitle("Global carbon price (USD/tCO2)", size($xytitle pt))              
>                                 ///
> ylabel(, labsize($xylab pt))                                             
>                                 ///
> xtitle("Temperature rise deemed acceptable (°C)", size($xytitle pt)  marg
> in(0 0 0 4))                    ///
> xlabel(1 `" "0°C" "(n=`n_1')" "' 2 `" "0.5°C" "(n=`n_2')" "'  3 `" "1°C" 
> "(n=`n_3')" "' 4 `" "1.5°C" "(n=`n_4')" "' 5 `" "2°C" "(n=`n_5')" "' 6 `"
>  "{&ge}2.5°C" "(n=`n_6')" "' , labsize(2.5 pt))                          
>                       ///
> legend(order(1 "Observation" 2 "Mean" 3 "Median") size($legend pt) rows(3
> ) pos(6) ring(1) region(fcolor(%40)))

    used)

. // Fig. 1b: Shifting the burden to other countries and the future (Descri
> ptives)
. preserve

. 
. ** Save number of observations per income-level in local
. forvalues i = 1/4 {
  2. sum income_level if income_level == `i'
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         50           1           0          1          1

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |        103           2           0          2          2

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         56           3           0          3          3

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         68           4           0          4          4

. 
. ** Collpase observations to receive median
. collapse (median) price_home_now price_oecd_now price_ldc_now price_home_
> future price_oecd_future price_ldc_future , by(income_level)

. 
. ** Reshaping dataset from wide to long
. foreach var in price_home price_oecd price_ldc {
  2. rename `var'_now `var'1
  3. rename `var'_future `var'2
  4. }

. reshape long price_home price_oecd price_ldc, i(income_level) j(now_futur
> e)
(note: j = 1 2)

Data                               wide   ->   long
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
> --
Number of obs.                        4   ->       8
Number of variables                   7   ->       5
j variable (2 values)                     ->   now_future
xij variables:
                price_home1 price_home2   ->   price_home
                price_oecd1 price_oecd2   ->   price_oecd
                  price_ldc1 price_ldc2   ->   price_ldc
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
> --

. lab define now_future 1 "Now" 2 "Future"

. lab val now_future now_future

. gen income_level_future = .
(8 missing values generated)

. replace income_level_future  = income_level if now_future == 1
(4 real changes made)

. replace income_level_future  = income_level + .25 if now_future == 2
(4 real changes made)

. 
. ** Draw figure
. global y = -6

. twoway ///
>         rspike price_home price_oecd income_level if now_future == 1, ver
> tical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538y%25) xlabel(0(25)150)          || /// Now
> : Home-OECD
>         rspike price_home price_ldc income_level if now_future == 1, vert
> ical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538bs1%25) xlabel(0(25)150)         || /// Now

> ure: Home-OECD

>  2, vertical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538bs1%25) xlabel(0(25)150) || /// Fut
> ure: Home-LDC
>     scatter price_ldc  income_level if now_future == 1,  mcolor(538bs1%80
> )           || /// Now: LDC
>         scatter price_home income_level if now_future == 1,  mcolor(538g%
> 80)             || /// Now: Home
>         scatter price_oecd income_level if now_future == 1,  mcolor(538y%
> 80)             || /// Now: OECD
>     scatter price_ldc  income_level_future if now_future == 2,  mcolor(53
> 8bs1%80)      || /// Future: LDC
>         scatter price_home income_level_future if now_future == 2,  mcolo
> r(538g%80)        || /// Future: Home
>         scatter price_oecd income_level_future if now_future == 2,  mcolo
> r(538y%80)        || /// Future: OECDw-Future: LDC, High
>     line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 1,  lcolor(538
> g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Low
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 2,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Low-Mid
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 3,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Upper-Mid
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 4,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash)    /// Now-Future: Home, High
>         title("{bf:b }", pos(11) span size($head pt))                    
>                                         ///
>         ytitle("Area-specific carbon price (median, in USD/tCO2)", size($
> xytitle pt))                            ///
>     ylabel(0 25 50 75 100 125 150, labsize($xylab pt) noticks nogrid) ymt
> ick(25 50 75 100 125 150, grid)     ///
>         yline(0, lcolor(gs12%40) lpattern(solid))                        
>                                         ///
>         xtitle(Income level (country), size($xytitle pt) margin(0 0 0 4))
>                                         ///
>         xlabel(1.125 `" "Low" "(n=`n_1')" "'  2.125 `" "Low-Mid" "(n=`n_2
> ')" "' 3.125 `" "Up-Mid" "(n=`n_3')" "' 4.125 `" "High" "(n=`n_4')" "', l
> absize(2.5 pt)) ///
>         ttext($y 1 "Now " $y 1.25 "Future" $y 2  "Now" $y 2.25 "Future" $
> y 3 "Now"  $y 3.25 "Future" $y 4 "Now" $y 4.25 "Future", orientation(vert
> ical) placement(north) color(gs10) size(7pt)) /// Y X "Text"  
>                 legend(order(5 "Price LDC" 2 "Diff LDC-Home" 6 "Price Hom
> e" 11 "Diff Home Now-Future" 7 "Price OECD" 3 "Diff Home-OECD") cols(2) p
> os(6) ring(1) size($legend pt) region(fcolor(%40))) graphregion(fcolor(no
> ne))

. // Generating variables

. // Sociodemographics
. ** Education
. tab edu, generate(edu)

     Field in which |
  highes degree was |
           obtained |      Freq.     Percent        Cum.

    Natural Science |        126       45.49       45.49
     Social Science |         55       19.86       65.34

         Type of organization |
        currently working for |      Freq.     Percent        Cum.
------------------------------+-----------------------------------

       Nat. Gov. Organization |        168       60.65       64.62
University/Research Institute |         33       11.91       76.53
              Private Company |          8        2.89       79.42
            Environmental NGO |         25        9.03       88.45
        Non-Environmental NGO |          6        2.17       90.61
                        Other |         26        9.39      100.00
------------------------------+-----------------------------------
                        Total |        277      100.00

. 
.

. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. ** Temperature above 1.5 degrees
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptabl
> e:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 
> 2.5°C or more are summarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2
> .5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Global carbon price suggested
. ** Logarithmic form of suggested carbon prices
. gen ln_carbon_price = ln(carbon_price + 1)

. label var ln_carbon_price "Natural logarithm of suggested carbon_price"

. 
. ** Cropping carbon price suggested at 500 for visualization in figure 1a
. gen carbon_price_cap = carbon_price

. replace carbon_price_cap  = 501 if carbon_price > 500
(23 real changes made)

. egen mean_carbon_price = mean(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. egen median_carbon_price = median(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. tab temp_rise_cropped , gen(tr)

  All those |
 suggesting |
2.5 or more |
  collected |
     in 2.5 |      Freq.     Percent        Cum.
------------+-----------------------------------
          0 |         22        7.94        7.94
         .5 |         36       13.00       20.94
          1 |         42       15.16       36.10
        1.5 |        116       41.88       77.98
          2 |         40       14.44       92.42
        2.5 |         21        7.58      100.00
------------+-----------------------------------
      Total |        277      100.00

. 
. ** Price suggested below 60 USD
. gen price_below = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace price_below = 0 if carbon_price >= 60 
(126 real changes made)

. replace price_below = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below "Price suggested < USD60"

. 
. /*
> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices to stay b
> elow a certain temperature rise. In the main paper we use USD60 as thte t
> hreshold. As robustness test, we also test against other specifications.
> */
. gen price_below_60 = 0

. replace price_below_60 = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_60 "Price below USD60 suggested"

. 
. gen price_below_185 = 0

. replace price_below_185 = 1 if carbon_price < 185 
(224 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_185 "Price below USD185 suggested"

. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Region- and time-specific carbon price suggestions
. ** Logarithms of prices suggested prices for home, OECD, LDC / now, futur
> e
. foreach var in price_home_now price_oecd_now price_ldc_now price_home_fut
> ure price_oecd_future price_ldc_future {
  2. gen ln_`var' = log(`var' + 1)
  3. }

. lab var ln_price_home_now "Ln of Price Home Now"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_now "Ln of Price OECD Now"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_now "Ln of Price LDCs Now"

. lab var ln_price_home_future "Ln of Price Home Future"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_future "Ln of Price OECD Future"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_future "Ln of Price LDCs Future"

. 
. ** Categorizing the ambitions of delegates for prices now and in the futu
> re
. gen ambition_home_fut = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 1 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future
>  < 60  // Low ambition
(148 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 2 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future
>  >= 60 // Shift to future
(50 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 3 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future
>  < 60  // Shift to now
(3 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 4 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future
>  >= 60 // High ambition
(76 real changes made)

. lab define ambition_fut 1 "Low ambition" 2 "Future pay more" 3 "Now pay m
> ore" 4 "High ambition", replace

. lab val ambition_home_fut ambition_fut

> ique

. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. ** Temperature above 1.5 degrees
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptabl
> e:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 
> 2.5°C or more are summarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2
> .5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Global carbon price suggested
. ** Logarithmic form of suggested carbon prices
. gen ln_carbon_price = ln(carbon_price + 1)

. label var ln_carbon_price "Natural logarithm of suggested carbon_price"

. 
. ** Cropping carbon price suggested at 500 for visualization in figure 1a
. gen carbon_price_cap = carbon_price

. replace carbon_price_cap  = 501 if carbon_price > 500
(23 real changes made)

. egen mean_carbon_price = mean(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. egen median_carbon_price = median(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. tab temp_rise_cropped , gen(tr)

  All those |
 suggesting |
2.5 or more |
  collected |
     in 2.5 |      Freq.     Percent        Cum.
------------+-----------------------------------
          0 |         22        7.94        7.94
         .5 |         36       13.00       20.94
          1 |         42       15.16       36.10
        1.5 |        116       41.88       77.98
          2 |         40       14.44       92.42
        2.5 |         21        7.58      100.00
------------+-----------------------------------
      Total |        277      100.00

. 
. ** Price suggested below 60 USD
. gen price_below = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace price_below = 0 if carbon_price >= 60 
(126 real changes made)

. replace price_below = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below "Price suggested < USD60"

. 
. /*
> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices to stay b
> elow a certain temperature rise. In the main paper we use USD60 as thte t
> hreshold. As robustness test, we also test against other specifications.
> */
. gen price_below_60 = 0

. replace price_below_60 = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_60 "Price below USD60 suggested"

. 
. gen price_below_185 = 0

. replace price_below_185 = 1 if carbon_price < 185 
(224 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_185 "Price below USD185 suggested"

. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Region- and time-specific carbon price suggestions
. ** Logarithms of prices suggested prices for home, OECD, LDC / now, futur
> e
. foreach var in price_home_now price_oecd_now price_ldc_now price_home_fut
> ure price_oecd_future price_ldc_future {
  2. gen ln_`var' = log(`var' + 1)
  3. }

. lab var ln_price_home_now "Ln of Price Home Now"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_now "Ln of Price OECD Now"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_now "Ln of Price LDCs Now"

. lab var ln_price_home_future "Ln of Price Home Future"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_future "Ln of Price OECD Future"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_future "Ln of Price LDCs Future"

. 
. ** Categorizing the ambitions of delegates for prices now and in the futu
> re
. gen ambition_home_fut = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 1 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future
>  < 60  // Low ambition
(148 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 2 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future
>  >= 60 // Shift to future
(50 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 3 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future
>  < 60  // Shift to now
(3 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 4 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future
>  >= 60 // High ambition
(76 real changes made)

. lab define ambition_fut 1 "Low ambition" 2 "Future pay more" 3 "Now pay m
> ore" 4 "High ambition", replace

. lab val ambition_home_fut ambition_fut

. 
. 
.

. do "C:\Users\MAXBUR~1\AppData\Local\Temp\STD5be8_000000.tmp"

. *--------------------------------------------------
. * Analysis.do

. /*
> Main Body:
> I)  Fig. 1: Descriptives
>         a) Carbon price and temperature rise
>         b) Shifting the burden

> II) Fig. 2: Inferential

. use "$working_ANALYSIS\data\delegates_analysis.dta", clear

. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. *---------------------------------------
. *   I) FIGURE 1: Temperature rise deemed acceptable, carbon price suggest
> ed, and negotiation strategy applied
. *------------------------------
. // Figure Settings
. * Text size
. global head     10 // Title

. global legend    8 // Legend

. global xytitle   8 // Axis title

. global xylab     8 // Scale label

. 
. 
. // Fig 1a: Stripplot: Price and temperature rise 
. * Generate variable defining position of observations on x-axis
. egen carbon_price_rank = rank(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropped) un
> ique

. egen temp_rise_cropped_freq = count(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropp
> ed)

. gen  temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 = temp_rise_cropped + (carbon_price_rank *
> .006) - (temp_rise_cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. 
. * Save number of observations in locals
. forvalues i = 1/6 {
  2. sum ln_carbon_price if tr`i' == 1
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         22    3.323065    2.261287          0   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         36    3.722019    2.127395   .6931472   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         42    4.207788    1.800718   1.098612   7.601402

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |        116    4.121002    1.359837          0   7.313887

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         40    3.659859    1.407166          0   6.552508

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
ln_carbon_~e |         21    3.544467    1.325008   .6931472   6.908755

. twoway ///
> (scatter carbon_price_cap temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 , mcolor(%30) msize(m
> edium) msymbol(o))              ///
> (scatter mean_carbon_price temp_rise_cropped , mcolor(538g) msymbol(trian
> gle))                                  ///
> (scatter median_carbon_price temp_rise_cropped , mcolor(538r) msymbol(squ
> are))                                  ///
> , title("{bf:a }", pos(11) span size($head pt))                          
>                                 ///
> ytitle("Global carbon price (USD/tCO2)", size($xytitle pt))              
>                                 ///
> ylabel(, labsize($xylab pt))                                             
>                                 ///
> xtitle("Temperature rise deemed acceptable (°C)", size($xytitle pt)  marg
> in(0 0 0 4))                    ///
> xlabel(1 `" "0°C" "(n=`n_1')" "' 2 `" "0.5°C" "(n=`n_2')" "'  3 `" "1°C" 
> "(n=`n_3')" "' 4 `" "1.5°C" "(n=`n_4')" "' 5 `" "2°C" "(n=`n_5')" "' 6 `"
>  "{&ge}2.5°C" "(n=`n_6')" "' , labsize(2.5 pt))                          
>                       ///
> legend(order(1 "Observation" 2 "Mean" 3 "Median") size($legend pt) rows(3
> ) pos(6) ring(1) region(fcolor(%40)))

. // Fig. 1b: Shifting the burden to other countries and the future (Descri
> ptives)
. preserve

. 
. ** Save number of observations per income-level in local
. forvalues i = 1/4 {
  2. sum income_level if income_level == `i'
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         50           1           0          1          1

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |        103           2           0          2          2

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         56           3           0          3          3

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------
income_level |         68           4           0          4          4

. 
. ** Collpase observations to receive median
. collapse (median) price_home_now price_oecd_now price_ldc_now price_home_
> future price_oecd_future price_ldc_future , by(income_level)

. 
. ** Reshaping dataset from wide to long
. foreach var in price_home price_oecd price_ldc {
  2. rename `var'_now `var'1
  3. rename `var'_future `var'2
  4. }

. reshape long price_home price_oecd price_ldc, i(income_level) j(now_futur
> e)
(note: j = 1 2)

Data                               wide   ->   long
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
> --
Number of obs.                        4   ->       8
Number of variables                   7   ->       5
j variable (2 values)                     ->   now_future
xij variables:
                price_home1 price_home2   ->   price_home
                price_oecd1 price_oecd2   ->   price_oecd
                  price_ldc1 price_ldc2   ->   price_ldc
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
> --

. lab define now_future 1 "Now" 2 "Future"

. lab val now_future now_future

. gen income_level_future = .
(8 missing values generated)

. replace income_level_future  = income_level if now_future == 1
(4 real changes made)

. replace income_level_future  = income_level + .25 if now_future == 2
(4 real changes made)

. 
. ** Draw figure
. global y = -6

. twoway ///
>         rspike price_home price_oecd income_level if now_future == 1, ver
> tical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538y%25) xlabel(0(25)150)          || /// Now
> : Home-OECD
>         rspike price_home price_ldc income_level if now_future == 1, vert
> ical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538bs1%25) xlabel(0(25)150)         || /// Now
> : Home-LDC
>         rspike price_home price_oecd income_level_future if now_future ==
>  2, vertical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538y%25) xlabel(0(25)150)   || /// Fut
> ure: Home-OECD
>         rspike price_home price_ldc income_level_future  if now_future ==
>  2, vertical lwidth(vthick) lcolor(538bs1%25) xlabel(0(25)150) || /// Fut
> ure: Home-LDC
>     scatter price_ldc  income_level if now_future == 1,  mcolor(538bs1%80
> )           || /// Now: LDC
>         scatter price_home income_level if now_future == 1,  mcolor(538g%
> 80)             || /// Now: Home
>         scatter price_oecd income_level if now_future == 1,  mcolor(538y%
> 80)             || /// Now: OECD
>     scatter price_ldc  income_level_future if now_future == 2,  mcolor(53
> 8bs1%80)      || /// Future: LDC
>         scatter price_home income_level_future if now_future == 2,  mcolo
> r(538g%80)        || /// Future: Home
>         scatter price_oecd income_level_future if now_future == 2,  mcolo
> r(538y%80)        || /// Future: OECDw-Future: LDC, High
>     line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 1,  lcolor(538
> g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Low
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 2,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Low-Mid
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 3,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Upper-Mid
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 4,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash)    /// Now-Future: Home, High
>         title("{bf:b }", pos(11) span size($head pt))                    
>                                         ///
>         ytitle("Area-specific carbon price (median, in USD/tCO2)", size($
> xytitle pt))                            ///
>     ylabel(0 25 50 75 100 125 150, labsize($xylab pt) noticks nogrid) ymt
> ick(25 50 75 100 125 150, grid)     ///
>         yline(0, lcolor(gs12%40) lpattern(solid))                        
>                                         ///
>         xtitle(Income level (country), size($xytitle pt) margin(0 0 0 4))
>                                         ///
>         xlabel(1.125 `" "Low" "(n=`n_1')" "'  2.125 `" "Low-Mid" "(n=`n_2
> ')" "' 3.125 `" "Up-Mid" "(n=`n_3')" "' 4.125 `" "High" "(n=`n_4')" "', l
> absize(2.5 pt)) ///
>         ttext($y 1 "Now " $y 1.25 "Future" $y 2  "Now" $y 2.25 "Future" $
> y 3 "Now"  $y 3.25 "Future" $y 4 "Now" $y 4.25 "Future", orientation(vert
> ical) placement(north) color(gs10) size(7pt)) /// Y X "Text"  
>                 legend(order(5 "Price LDC" 2 "Diff LDC-Home" 6 "Price Hom
> e" 11 "Diff Home Now-Future" 7 "Price OECD" 3 "Diff Home-OECD") cols(2) p
> os(6) ring(1) size($legend pt) region(fcolor(%40))) graphregion(fcolor(no
> ne))

. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. ** Temperature above 1.5 degrees
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptabl
> e:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 
> 2.5°C or more are summarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2
> .5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. 
. 
. 
. 
. 
. // Global carbon price suggested
. ** Logarithmic form of suggested carbon prices
. gen ln_carbon_price = ln(carbon_price + 1)

. label var ln_carbon_price "Natural logarithm of suggested carbon_price"

. 
. ** Cropping carbon price suggested at 500 for visualization in figure 1a
. gen carbon_price_cap = carbon_price

. replace carbon_price_cap  = 501 if carbon_price > 500
(23 real changes made)

. egen mean_carbon_price = mean(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. egen median_carbon_price = median(carbon_price), by(temp_rise_cropped)

. tab temp_rise_cropped , gen(tr)

. ** Price suggested below 60 USD
. gen price_below = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace price_below = 0 if carbon_price >= 60 
(126 real changes made)

. replace price_below = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below "Price suggested < USD60"

. 
. /*
> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices to stay b
> elow a certain temperature rise. In the main paper we use USD60 as thte t
> hreshold. As robustness test, we also test against other specifications.
> */
. gen price_below_60 = 0

. replace price_below_60 = 1 if carbon_price < 60 
(151 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_60 "Price below USD60 suggested"

. 
. gen price_below_185 = 0

. replace price_below_185 = 1 if carbon_price < 185 
(224 real changes made)

. lab var price_below_185 "Price below USD185 suggested"

. // Region- and time-specific carbon price suggestions
. ** Logarithms of prices suggested prices for home, OECD, LDC / now, futur
> e
. foreach var in price_home_now price_oecd_now price_ldc_now price_home_fut
> ure price_oecd_future price_ldc_future {
  2. gen ln_`var' = log(`var' + 1)
  3. }

. lab var ln_price_home_now "Ln of Price Home Now"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_now "Ln of Price OECD Now"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_now "Ln of Price LDCs Now"

. lab var ln_price_home_future "Ln of Price Home Future"

. lab var ln_price_oecd_future "Ln of Price OECD Future"

. lab var ln_price_ldc_future "Ln of Price LDCs Future"

. 
. ** Categorizing the ambitions of delegates for prices now and in the futu
> re
. gen ambition_home_fut = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 1 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future
>  < 60  // Low ambition
(148 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 2 if price_home_now < 60  & price_home_future
>  >= 60 // Shift to future
(50 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 3 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future
>  < 60  // Shift to now
(3 real changes made)

. replace ambition_home_fut = 4 if price_home_now >= 60 & price_home_future
>  >= 60 // High ambition
(76 real changes made)

. lab define ambition_fut 1 "Low ambition" 2 "Future pay more" 3 "Now pay m
> ore" 4 "High ambition", replace

. lab val ambition_home_fut ambition_fut

.

. // Temperature rise deemed acceptable
. ** Temperature above 1.5 degrees
. gen temp_above = .
(277 missing values generated)

. replace temp_above = 0 if temp_rise <= 1.5
(216 real changes made)

. replace temp_above = 1 if temp_rise > 1.5
(61 real changes made)

. lab var temp_above "Temperature rise above 1.5°C deemed acceptable"

. 
. /*
> Very few people suggested temperatures of 2.5°C or higher to be acceptabl
> e:
> 2.5°C -> 9
> 3.0°C -> 4
> 3.5°C -> 2
> 4.0°C -> 2
> 4.5°C -> 0
> 5.0°C -> 4
> Therefore, for the illustration Figure 1a all temperature suggestions of 
> 2.5°C or more are summarized under >= 2.5°C
> */
. gen temp_rise2 = temp_rise

. replace temp_rise2 = 2.5 if temp_rise >= 2.5
(12 real changes made)

. tostring temp_rise2, gen(temp_rise3)
temp_rise3 generated as str3

. sort temp_rise

. lab define temp 1 "0" 2 ".5" 3 "1" 4 "1.5", replace

. encode temp_rise3, gen(temp_rise_cropped) lab(temp)

. lab var temp_rise_cropped"All those suggesting 2.5 or more collected in 2
> .5"

. drop temp_rise2 temp_rise3

. ** Price suggested below 60 USD

. lab var price_below "Price suggested < USD60"

. 
. /*
> Carbon price suggestions tested
> Different models suggest different minimal global carbon prices to stay b
> elow a certain temperature rise. In the main paper we use USD60 as thte t
> hreshold. As robustness test, we also test against other specifications: 
> 82 USD, 185 USD, 281 USD
> */
. foreach i in 60 82 185 281 {
  2.         gen price_below_`i' = .
  3.                 replace price_below_`i'= 1 if carbon_price < `i'
  4.                 replace price_below_`i'= 0 if carbon_price >=  `i'
  5.         lab var price_below_`i' "Price below USD `i' suggested"
  6. }
(277 missing values generated)

(277 missing values generated)
(175 real changes made)

(277 missing values generated)

(53 real changes made)

. /*
> Main Body:
> I)  Fig. 1: Descriptives
>         a) Carbon price and temperature rise
>         b) Shifting the burden

>         a) Answers towards technological optimism items

> ted

> III) In text-statistics not mentioned in the supplementary online materia
> l
>     - "Delegates vastly agree to limit global warming: The majority perce
> ives a rise above 1.5°C unacceptable (78%), with only few (8%) deeming an
>  increase of 2.5°C or more acceptable."
>     - "The median global carbon price recommended in our sample is 50 USD
>  [...]"
>     - "Roughly half of all delegates interviewed stated rather unambitiou
> s carbon prices below 60 USD (55%). Only 37% (19% and 13%, respectively) 
> deemed a price of at least 82 USD (185 USD, 281 USD) as appropriate"
>     - "This variance in global price suggested is highest for the three l
> ow temperature options (0°C, 0.5°C and 1°C), with price suggestions rangi
> ng from 0 to 2,000 USD (Levene’s test F(1, 275)=21.7, p<0.001)."
>     - "Of the 100 delegates [suggesting prices between 0°C und 1°C] in fa
> vor of these ambitious temperature targets, 62% indicated global carbon p
> rices below 60 USD as appropriate to stay below the temperature target."
>     - "In addition, we find that participants who claim to be influential
>  in their delegation score higher on the technological optimism mindset (
> r=.23, p<.001)."
> */

. use "$working_ANALYSIS\data\delegates_analysis.dta", clear

. *   I) FIGURE 1: Temperature rise deemed acceptable, carbon price suggest
> ed, and negotiation strategy applied

. // Fig 1a: Stripplot: Price and temperature rise 
. * Generate variable defining position of observations on x-axis
. egen carbon_price_rank = rank(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropped) un
> ique

. egen temp_rise_cropped_freq = count(carbon_price_cap), by(temp_rise_cropp
> ed)

. gen  temp_rise_cropped_jitter2 = temp_rise_cropped + (carbon_price_rank *
> .006) - (temp_rise_cropped_freq / 2 * 0.006)

. 
. * Save number of observations in locals
. forvalues i = 1/6 {
  2. sum ln_carbon_price if tr`i' == 1
  3. local n_`i' = r(N)
  4. }

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max
-------------+---------------------------------------------------------

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max

    Variable |        Obs        Mean    Std. Dev.       Min        Max

>  "{&ge}2.5°C" "(n=`n_6')" "' , labsize(2.5 pt))

  4. }

> future price_oecd_future price_ldc_future , by(income_level)

. ** Reshaping dataset from wide to long

  2. rename `var'_now `var'1
  3. rename `var'_future `var'2
  4. }

. reshape long price_home price_oecd price_ldc, i(income_level) j(now_futur
> e)
(note: j = 1 2)

Data                               wide   ->   long
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
> --
Number of obs.                        4   ->       8
Number of variables                   7   ->       5
j variable (2 values)                     ->   now_future
xij variables:
                price_home1 price_home2   ->   price_home
                price_oecd1 price_oecd2   ->   price_oecd
                  price_ldc1 price_ldc2   ->   price_ldc
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
> --

. lab define now_future 1 "Now" 2 "Future"

. lab val now_future now_future

. gen income_level_future = .
(8 missing values generated)

. replace income_level_future  = income_level if now_future == 1
(4 real changes made)

. replace income_level_future  = income_level + .25 if now_future == 2
(4 real changes made)

> 80)             || /// Now: OECD

> 8bs1%80)      || /// Future: LDC

> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Low-Mid
>         line price_home income_level_future if income_level == 3,  lcolor
> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash) || /// Now-Future: Home, Upper-Mid

> (538g%40)  lpattern(dash)    /// Now-Future: Home, High
>         title("{bf:b }", pos(11) span size($head pt))

> absize(2.5 pt)) ///

> o.com

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 co2_emissionpc

. label var co2_emissionpc "CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)"

. 
. drop average2 // no values for countries in dataset

. 
. rename average3 gdp

. label var gdp "GDP (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average4 gdp_growth

. label var gdp_growth "GDP growth (annual %)"

. 
. rename average5 gdppc

. label var gdppc "GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average6 population

. label var population "Population, total"

. 
. 
. 
. * Unify country names
. replace country_home = "Congo" if country_home == "Congo, Rep."
(1 real change made)

. replace country_home = "Czechia" if country_home == "Czech Republic"
(1 real change made)

. replace country_home = "Democratic Republic of the Congo" if country_home == "
> Congo, Dem. Rep."
(1 real change made)

. /*
> Three participants answered the survey twice; same e-mail adress twice in data
> set. For each couple, same name&lastname:
> 
> Date            firstname                               lastname              
>   email
> 04.11.2020      Ram Prasad                              Awasthi               
>   awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi       
>           awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 
> 02.12.2020      Nagla                                   Jebory                
>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com
> 05.11.2020      Nagla Mahgoub Hamadain  Jebory                  nagla_fnc@yaho
> o.com
> 
> 06.11.2020      Augustin                                Ngenzirabona    augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 25.03.2021      Ngenzirablna                    Augustin                augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 
> Keep first entry of each
> */
. drop if firstname == "Ram" & lastname == "Awasthi"
(1 observation deleted)

. drop if firstname == "Nagla Mahgoub Hamadain" & lastname == "Jebory"
(1 observation deleted)

. drop if firstname == "Ngenzirablna" & lastname == "Augustin"
(1 observation deleted)

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 co2_emissionpc

. label var co2_emissionpc "CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)"

. 
. drop average2 // no values for countries in dataset

. 
. rename average3 gdp

. label var gdp "GDP (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average4 gdp_growth

. label var gdp_growth "GDP growth (annual %)"

. 
. rename average5 gdppc

. label var gdppc "GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average6 population

. label var population "Population, total"

. 
. 
.

> o.com

> enzi@yahoo.fr

> enzi@yahoo.fr

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 co2_emissionpc

. label var co2_emissionpc "CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)"

. 
. drop average2 // no values for countries in dataset

. 
. rename average3 gdp

. label var gdp "GDP (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average4 gdp_growth

. label var gdp_growth "GDP growth (annual %)"

. 
. rename average5 gdppc

. label var gdppc "GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average6 population

. label var population "Population, total"

. 
. 
. 
. * Unify country names
. replace country_home = "Congo" if country_home == "Congo, Rep."
(1 real change made)

. replace country_home = "Czechia" if country_home == "Czech Republic"
(1 real change made)

. replace country_home = "Democratic Republic of the Congo" if country_home == "
> Congo, Dem. Rep."
(1 real change made)

. replace country_home = "Egypt" if country_home == "Egypt, Arab Rep."
(1 real change made)

>

>   awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi       
>           awasthiramprasad@gmail.com

>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com

> o.com
>

> enzi@yahoo.fr

> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 
> Keep first entry of each
> */

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 co2_emissionpc

. label var co2_emissionpc "CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)"

. 
. drop average2 // no values for countries in dataset

. 
. rename average3 gdp

. label var gdp "GDP (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average4 gdp_growth

. label var gdp_growth "GDP growth (annual %)"

. 
. rename average5 gdppc

. label var gdppc "GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average6 population

. label var population "Population, total"

. 
. 
. 
. * Unify country names
. replace country_home = "Congo" if country_home == "Congo, Rep."
(1 real change made)

. /*
> Three participants answered the survey twice; same e-mail adress twice in data
> set. For each couple, same name&lastname:
> 
> Date            firstname                               lastname              
>   email
> 04.11.2020      Ram Prasad                              Awasthi               
>   awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 16.02.2021      Ram                                             Awasthi       
>           awasthiramprasad@gmail.com
> 
> 02.12.2020      Nagla                                   Jebory                
>   nagla_fnc@yahoo.com
> 05.11.2020      Nagla Mahgoub Hamadain  Jebory                  nagla_fnc@yaho
> o.com
> 
> 06.11.2020      Augustin                                Ngenzirabona    augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 25.03.2021      Ngenzirablna                    Augustin                augung
> enzi@yahoo.fr
> 
> Keep first entry of each
> */

(1 observation deleted)

(1 observation deleted)

. * IV) Merge country-specifics

. // World development indices
. *import excel "$xls\WDI_Indexes_average 2015-2019", sheet("Sheet1") firstrow c
> ase(lower) clear
. 
. import excel "$xls\Data_Extract_From_World_Development_Indicators", sheet("Dat
> a") firstrow case(lower) clear
(9 vars, 1,601 obs)

. foreach var in yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019 {
  2. replace `var' = "." if `var' == ".."
  3. }
(325 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(333 real changes made)
(336 real changes made)
(581 real changes made)

. destring yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019, replace
yr2015: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(330 missing values generated)
yr2016: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2017: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(338 missing values generated)
yr2018: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(341 missing values generated)
yr2019: all characters numeric; replaced as double
(586 missing values generated)

. encode countrycode, generate(country_code)

. egen average = rowmean(yr2015 yr2016 yr2017 yr2018 yr2019)
(329 missing values generated)

. keep countryname average seriesname

. drop if countryname == ""
(3 observations deleted)

. 
. * Reshape to wide
. egen indicator = group(seriesname)
(2 missing values generated)

. drop if indicator == . // Datasource information
(2 observations deleted)

. 
. /* 
> 1: CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)       
> 2: Droughts, floods, extreme temperatures (% of population, average 1990-2009)
> 3: GDP (constant 2015 US$); 
> 4: GDP growth (annual %)
> 5: GDP per capita (constant 2015 US$)
> 6: Population, total
> */
. 
. drop seriesname 

. encode countryname , gen(country_code)

. reshape wide average , i(country_code) j(indicator)
(note: j = 1 2 3 4 5 6)

Data                               long   ->   wide
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Number of obs.                     1596   ->     266
Number of variables                   4   ->       8
j variable (6 values)         indicator   ->   (dropped)
xij variables:
                                average   ->   average1 average2 ... average6
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

. 
. * Unify variable names
. rename countryname country_home

. label var country_home "Home country"

. drop country_code

. order country_home

. 
. rename average1 co2_emissionpc

. label var co2_emissionpc "CO2 emissions (metric tons per capita)"

. 
. drop average2 // no values for countries in dataset

. 
. rename average3 gdp

. label var gdp "GDP (constant 2015 US$)"

. 
. rename average4 gdp_growth

. label var gdp_growth "GDP growth (annual %)"

. 
. rename average5 gdppc
